<Text>I lived here for more than seven years.  They were to have given me the entire deposit back (California statute) due to the amount of time I lived there.  They did not.  I considered taking them to small claims court but ended up not following through (which was my fault but I just wanted to be done with it).

Then I got a phone call - Hey, you owe us money from the move out. I gave the person an ear-full, let them know that I didn't receive my deposit that I was entitled to (by law, mind you), and that I was owed money not the other way around.

This would have been the end of it....until I got ANOTHER phone call YEARS later (four years later, to be exact) asking me about the money I "owed". *sigh*.  I had to explain to that lady what the deal was (apparently she was newly hired, had gone through the files to be a diligent worker, and unilaterally decided to follow-up on my file in order to be a good worker bee; bless her heart).  She was caught like a deer in a headlights at my response, although I was not rude nor was I even mad at that point just amazed at the lack of organization by management.

DOCUMENT EVERYTHING!  Take pictures when you move in, and take pictures when you move out!  Video tape the walk through at move in and at move out.  Make sure they provide an itemized list that details what the costs were in case they do not give your whole deposit back!

Back when I lived here, car break-ins were extremely frequent (it was only a matter of time before you car got broken into, almost like a rite of passage in becoming a resident here).  Management didn't care.  And there was a maintenance man that appeared to be a nice guy (though a bit rough around the edges) that ended up getting arrested because he was using the master key to enter apartments and steal stuff.

Our place was burglarized because it was right next to Barstow (due to the amount of foot traffic, I presume).  My neighbors next door were burglarized several times; there were a couple of guys that lived there that were victimized, and later on a girl who lived there that had to live through a very scary home invasion type burglary/robbery.

Just another day at the Plazas.

Were there good times?  Of course.  This was, however, in SPITE of management (not because of them).  The biggest plus about this complex is that it is close to Fresno State campus.  Beyond that?  PLEASE BE CAREFUL!</Text>< Pictures>

< review>
Today was my first time trying this place and I'm glad I did.  I ordered the tropical tea with fresh fruit and added the honey boba to it.  The tea was really good and clean tasting, and the honey boba was soft and fresh. The ONLY reason why I didn't give them 5 stars was because the amount of fresh fruit in my drink DID NOT match the advertised picture.  Mine had scarce bits and pieces floating around in it disguised with leaves and lemon.  Also, I'm not sure how slivers of strawberries and lemon are considered TROPICAL........... sound likes strawberry lemonade to me.  However, the tea was still tasty, so I will give them another try.<//review>

< Text>
This review is for Sprint generally in the Bay Area; Sprint worked fine for us in another city. We moved to the area and found the service was terrible here (dropped calls, missed calls, very poor voice quality, and frequent "no signal" readings). When we asked the Sprint customer service about cancelation they directed us to go to a Sprint store in-person to get our phones checked out. Long story short, after hours wasted with customer service we canceled with a full cancelation fee. If you go with Sprint in this area, check beforehand to see how coverage will be for you. Be ready to either deal with poor coverage or pay a full cancelation fee to switch out to something better. We are now on Project Fi and it the connection is consistently very good.< /Text>

< Text>
This place is a DUMP. People discard their trash like it was a landfill (it is).  The recycling section (breathable air) has places for wood, appliances, metals, inert solids, plastics and lots of dumptsters for trash, too. You go up to the landfill on top if you want to dump and go. The sign says "Dead Animals $70 a ton". Not real sure if they were buying or selling "mystery meats".  They weigh your truck on the way in and out, but I have never been charged. No scavenging unless you are a seagull or crow.< /Text>

< Review>
It's beautiful here. They've got a few picnic tables and nice clean restrooms. The trails are in excellent condition and range from easy to very difficult. However, it was windy and cold when we went which is not unusual for this area. It's also close to Pioneertown which is a nice bonus and it's only a few miles from two major highways. But be careful, the last mile or two are on a dirt road. The road wasn't too bad though. My 2-wheel drive car has low profile tires and sits pretty low and I didn't have any trouble getting there.< /Review>

< Review>
This was my first time ever to Sushi Delight and let me tell you, I am a life long fan! I enjoyed their Calamari Tempura Roll and their Lexus Roll and the Shrimp Tempura Roll. I even tried the Dynamite Roll! Each roll was so fresh and delicious! The rolls are so good you don't even need to dip them into any sauces.
Jerry was running the show there at Sushi Delight and he had a relationship with just about everyone who walked into the restaurant to pick up their order. It's refreshing to go somewhere that cares about more than making a profit off of you.
Let me share that I enjoyed it so much at lunchtime, that I went back for dinner that same day!!! It was awesome that they were offering 20 percent off specialty rolls that day too!
I will be visiting real soon to calm the craving I have had since visiting Sushi Delight!</Review>

1520310002825<//time>
<Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
IMO, best sushi in the South Bay. For the exceptional quality of fish and customer service, the price is more than fair.  I would definitely say that the customer is getting the better end of the deal. Comfortable and cozy, a great place for a date or lunch with friends. Service is always quick and I can usually grab a quick but great lunch. Normally I'm in and out within 35 minutes for lunch. This place is so good that I almost don't want to write this so it doesn't become too crowded, but I'm going to keep going anyway!

I'm not well versed on the Japanese terminology, but the sushi that is just rice and fish is by far the best I've had in the South Bay. The quality of their salmon sushi is exceptional. It is well marbled and almost buttery to the taste. The texture of the rice that they use is perfect, just enough of a bite to add texture but not overbearing or dry.

Their sushi rolls are also wonderful. My favorite is the Harley Davidson roll, which is a wonderfully tempura fried roll that has salmon and cream cheese in it, with other delicious things inside and out to add to the rich creaminess. Sounds a bit odd on paper, but it is a very unique and savory roll.

Great small place tucked away behind other mediocre businesses. Seriously, come and check it out, you'll be hard pressed to be let down.<//review>
